  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app',

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2539775874" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17789366232107233648">Jared Paterski is off to college and cannot wait to meet his new roommate. When he meets Alexander Schmidt, he could not be more delighted and decides Alex is for him. He likes him so much that he decides to dress and act like him, taking on some of his likes and dislikes. Jared has a lot of money and is not afraid to use it or not. He buys Alex expensive gifts and, then, introduces him to love and BDSM through his special dungeon.<br/><br/>I found Jared to be a bit annoying with how he talks about his mo</span>
  <span id="freeText17789366232107233648" style="display:none">Jared Paterski is off to college and cannot wait to meet his new roommate. When he meets Alexander Schmidt, he could not be more delighted and decides Alex is for him. He likes him so much that he decides to dress and act like him, taking on some of his likes and dislikes. Jared has a lot of money and is not afraid to use it or not. He buys Alex expensive gifts and, then, introduces him to love and BDSM through his special dungeon.<br /><br />I found Jared to be a bit annoying with how he talks about his money. He still, however, had the same insecurities and the same needs as any other young man going off to college. Alex was a first baffled by Jared and his money. He did, however, enthusiastically enjoy losing his innocence by participating in Jared's dungeon activities. The story did not end on a happy note but it is a series and now I cannot wait for the next book.</span>

<div id="review_2572413009" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2572413009" />
    <a title="Nova Caine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/88450826-nova-caine"><img alt="Nova Caine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1540416344p2/88450826.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2572413009?book_show_action=true">Oct 24, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nova Caine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nova Caine" href="/user/show/88450826-nova-caine">Nova Caine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/88450826-nova-caine?shelf=lgbt">lgbt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/88450826-nova-caine?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2572413009" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15387030388706568493">So this story is about two college students Jared Pasterski, and Alexander Schmidt who likes to go by Alex. Jared is attracted to Alex in every way possible. He likes everything about him and decides to live like him. He is insanely rich and spoils him with various items and gifts.   <span id="freeText280118306623236989" style="display:none">I'm not going to start on the how well this is written since that part did not really stand out to me but the overall story is what got me hooked on it. Here you have a story from a billionaire college (I've never heard of such) student named Jared Paterski, who is <i>very</i> (borderline obsessively...) attracted to this somewhat introverted athletic college student named Alexander Schmidt (hense the title) who happens to be his roommate. The way he likes him is in a way thats hard for me to describe, its much different than any other romance novel I've read, or with any relationship I've experienced. Jared is attracted to Alex so much that he has the desire to copy him to like him. I'm not sure how I feel about that, I've never seen a plot like that before, it's interesting nonetheless. But as soon as I got finished with the first chapter, I knew by the tone that there was going to be sex. <br><br><a href="https://imgur.com/hPUs1Gc" rel="nofollow noopener">

I sure wish my man would do that :). Although I wouldn't imagine two "average" college roommates doing this in real life, I think the author did a good job making it work for this story.<br><br><br>The only thing thats preventing me from giving this five stars is the over use of the terms "oh my" and Jared referring to his "inner sexual desires". Ok, I get it, Jared is a horny man just like many other college men but there could have been better ways to describe it.<br><br>Now to get to my final thoughts, I would recommend this book for anybody looking for a fun ;) &amp; fast read. It's sexy and unique.</span>

  <span id="freeText6954372524170026296" style="display:none">I want this to start off by saying that my intention isn't to hurt you, try to upset you, or troll you. I made an account on this site because I read a few chapters of your book and I couldn't read anymore. You tend to use the same phrases over and over (the one off the top of my head is "inner sexual desires" sprinkled 3-4 times each chapter). A little variety would go a long way! The flow of the sexual encounters is also really weird. It isn't very natural, and this reads more as like a high school fanfiction than a "novel". The whole aspect of having Jared copy Alexander's interests and everything to be like him is kind of unsettling if you were to think about this from a real-life perspective. And Alex who had never been with another male before seemed very knowledgeable in how to “reciprocate” Alex’s inner sexual desires, if you know what I mean. But it all worked somehow in all it’s quirkiness and I started missing the aforementioned phrase when it wasn’t mentioned on each page, lol. In fact I enjoyed it so much that before I was finished I immediately 1-clicked the follow up book. I’m so glad I did because there was a twist that I wasn’t expecting at the end, I gotta know what happens!</span>
  <a data-text-id="17213316758347112064" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2436470866" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2436470866" />
    <a title="Qin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66757539-qin"><img alt="Qin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1494117078p2/66757539.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2436470866?book_show_action=true">Jun 26, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Qin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Qin" href="/user/show/66757539-qin">Qin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2436470866" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3348271479034713957">By no means a bad BDSM novel, even if the writing could have been more fluent and stylish (it only gets inventive when the two protagonists engage into a scene); I especially enjoyed the tight balance between domination / submission and sexual gratification, especially for the bottom, two aspects that tend to get blurry in many stories purporting to illustrate this lifestyle. What ruined the book for me was a) the extremely fake context of the college for the ultra-rich, not only because it soun</span>
  <span id="freeText3348271479034713957" style="display:none">By no means a bad BDSM novel, even if the writing could have been more fluent and stylish (it only gets inventive when the two protagonists engage into a scene); I especially enjoyed the tight balance between domination / submission and sexual gratification, especially for the bottom, two aspects that tend to get blurry in many stories purporting to illustrate this lifestyle. What ruined the book for me was a) the extremely fake context of the college for the ultra-rich, not only because it sounds nigh preposterous but also since it reminded me of a silly old cartoon which I have trouble equating with such dirty, MM goodness as there is between these covers (viz. the campy, ultra cute <i>Beverly Hills Teens</i>); b) the oversimplistic plot, or rather its absence altogether, even as a peg on which Mrs Hanson hangs her numerous bedroom and domination interludes; and c) the slapdash psychological portrayal of the protagonists, which robbed me of most of my enjoyment (it is never stated, let alone convincingly shown, what deep needs Alexander satisfies by submitting to the creepily manipulative Jared). In my view, BDSM ought to be written in such fashion as to demonstrate through deeds and dialogue alike how exactly this lifestyle indulged into with the right person actually makes one happy and really satisfied; otherwise, the main danger is that the Dom comes across as hardly more than a controlling bastard-slash-pervert sadist, especially whenever this character has been established from the start as someone rather dark and twisted and emotionally stunted who lavishes money or status or whatever trappings at hand on his victim, er Submissive, instead of offering them the loving praise their power transfer deserves. I am afraid the present novel signally fails to cover its tracks in this respect.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3348271479034713957" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2794080440" />
    <a title="Maria Taylor" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/96324202-maria-taylor"><img alt="Maria Taylor" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2794080440?book_show_action=true">Apr 21, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maria Taylor" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maria Taylor" href="/user/show/96324202-maria-taylor">Maria Taylor</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2794080440" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1275604756261831537"><b>4.5 stars</b><br/><br/>I usually don't read M/M that much but I saw this book on my friends TBR list and I knew I had to check it out. This is a sexual love story that involves two college roommates Jared and Alex who quickly fall in love with some interesting characteristics. And by interesting, I mean not something I see in other love stories and that is the antagonist copying the protagonist in many ways such as interests and other identifying traits. There is a lot of sex and in many erotica novels I've r</span>
  <span id="freeText1275604756261831537" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars</b><br /><br />I usually don't read M/M that much but I saw this book on my friends TBR list and I knew I had to check it out. This is a sexual love story that involves two college roommates Jared and Alex who quickly fall in love with some interesting characteristics. And by interesting, I mean not something I see in other love stories and that is the antagonist copying the protagonist in many ways such as interests and other identifying traits. There is a lot of sex and in many erotica novels I've read, usually the scenes don't tie into the story (no pun intended lol) but in this story they do. While it's not said, I believe that each sex scene plays a huge role in their romantic relationship which is ultimately what caused me to keep reading. Not only was the sex hot, but the characters were also cute and smoldering in their descriptions. I really liked that the descriptions of the characters are very realistic and not some obviously fake characteristics that I've encountered in other books. <br /><br />Disclaimer: don't click the spoiler button if you haven't read the book yet.<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ One thing that actually got me by surprise is the ending where Alex runs away from Jared. Their relationship was pretty fluent and going well up to the end. This of which gave it a nice kick to the plot, and such I cannot wait to read the rest of the trilogy  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Nonetheless, I really adored the book and will certainty read it again. I also bought the other books of the trilogy, as well as Mister Soccer Player. *reviews of those coming soon!*</span>
  <a data-text-id="1275604756261831537" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText8303512530431024798" style="display:none">The book description was so promising and an interesting idea that only went downhill from there. The wording and the flow(or lack thereof) was truly atrocious. This does read like a wattpad story that should've stay there until it was edited and revised. The characters are talking as if they are reading from a scrip of a low-budget movie. I can read insta-love and enjoy it but this book takes the cake. Also, the repetive phrases and words killed me everytime. <br />For example: his sexy abs, his sexiness, and my inner sexual desires.<br />Also, the scene where he gives Alex the list is weird and then reads it to him is pretty cringeworthy. If I were Alex I would take the list and report it to the Dean. The way Jared kept touching his lips was also terrible; I've only known you for 2 days why are you: touching me inappropriately, following me, giving me expensive guests, and giving me a sex list? The book definitely tried but I wished that it had had a better review and editing process.</span>

I really enjoyed the story of 50SOG so it wasn't a surprise to me that I would enjoy this one as well. Despite the overwhelming amount </span>
  <span id="freeText10907101383158151733" style="display:none">At first I thought that the idea of having the story being about two college roommates would be kind of odd and unfitting, considering roommates are forced to live with each other, but it very much worked out. This story greatly reminds me of Fifty Shades of Grey with the erotic tones of BDSM, the list he has Alex read similar to the contract in 50SOG and so on. I really enjoyed the story of 50SOG so it wasn't a surprise to me that I would enjoy this one as well. Despite the overwhelming amount of sex scenes, which some people may prefer, I did enjoy the tight bond between the characters. At first, it seemed to me that Jared was trying to buy Alex with all of money and gifts and dinners, but later on, it seemed like he truly wanted him. Also, seeing the same story told in Alex's point of view in the second half was very intriguing as well. I know the love at first sight trope as been used in a LOT, understatement lol, of other romance novels but this one is one I enjoyed more than others. One thing that puzzled me is the fact that Jared had the desire to want to be like Alex. This isn't something that you wouldn't see in any other relationships. Yes, I do think the writing could be improved but I really enjoyed the story in the end.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10907101383158151733" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('A35dgg0tJa4J8f8XCXFqTqT3oIU8wtA3nlcjlGt+YExpwM5G+Zo0k5T/OtiGqz2bXJGKvOZXeu3cDc13wUkcqA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('2zk/reRYfcaiQrO41UPlyQg1Ly9nVVvmumKgkthoTPGxh6xpEO9s+z9MdndambIc8FMFFr3A8Tz4OE5xcl8wFQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
